#MODIFIED
@resolution_weight_hated = 3
@resolution_weight_disliked = 4
@resolution_weight_unpopular = 5
@resolution_weight_normal = 6
@resolution_weight_popular = 6.5
@resolution_weight_loved = 7

@resolution_cost_t1 = 100
@resolution_cost_t2 = 150
@resolution_cost_t3 = 200
@resolution_cost_t4 = 250
@resolution_cost_t5 = 300
@resolution_cost_denounce = 25

@resolution_flag_timer = 360

#example_resolution = {
#	icon = "name of the icon key"
#	resources = {} # cost and category
#	target = yes/no # if this resolution requires a target country
#	harmful = yes/no # if the AI should consider this harmful when choosing target
#	modifier = {} # modifier to be applied to all community members if passed
#	fire_and_forget = yes/no # if "yes", the resolution will not be added to the list of active/passed resolutions. Mainly used for repeal resolutions. Default: no
#	triggered_modifier = {} # triggered modifier to be applied, scope is country
#	effect = {} # effect to be applied if passed, scope is proposer unless there is a target country - then scope is target country, with proposer in from scope
#	fail_effects = {} # effect to be applied if failed, scope is proposer unless there is a target country - then scope is target country, with proposer in from scope
#	potential = {} # potential trigger, scope is country
#	allow = {} # allow trigger, scope is country
#	active = {} # Enacted resolutions are cancelled if this trigger fails
#
#	ai_weight = {} # ai weight modifiers, scope is country. from scope is the target country for targeted resolutions
#	NOTE: all ai_weight modifiers are multiplicative. The end result is also multiplied with a factor based on the opinion towards the proposer and/or target,
#	see RESOLUTION_TARGET_OPINION_MIN_FACTOR etc. in 00_defines.txt. Also see RESOLUTION_VOTE_SUPPORT_THRESHOLD etc. for balancing the values.
#
#	valid_target = {} # valid targets trigger, scope is country
#}

# NOTE: Remember to add Resolutions to a Resolution Category!

# Ecology

resolution_ecology_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_repeal_1_effect_success

		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_environmentalist = yes
			desc = gal_com_environment_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_terraformer = yes
			desc = gal_com_terraforming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
			desc = eco_trait_clean 
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
			desc = eco_trait_dirty
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_capitalist = yes
			desc = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			is_civic_plant_organic = yes
			desc = civic_plant_organic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
			desc = gal_com_miner_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			country_uses_food = yes
			desc = gal_com_country_uses_food_no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_lithoid_empire  = yes
			desc = lithoid
		}
	}
}

resolution_ecology_repeal_2 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_repeal_2_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_environmentalist = yes
			desc = gal_com_environment_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_terraformer = yes
			desc = gal_com_terraforming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
			desc = eco_trait_clean 
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
			desc = eco_trait_dirty
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_capitalist = yes
			desc = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_civic_plant_organic = yes
			desc = civic_plant_organic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_civic_functional_architecture = yes
			desc = civic_functional_architecture
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
			desc = gal_com_miner_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			country_uses_food = yes
			desc = gal_com_country_uses_food_no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_lithoid_empire  = yes
			desc = lithoid
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries
			desc = gal_com_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_ecology_repeal_3 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_repeal_3_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens_tooltip
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
		resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_environmentalist = yes
			desc = gal_com_environment_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_terraformer = yes
			desc = gal_com_terraforming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
			desc = eco_trait_clean 
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
			desc = eco_trait_dirty
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_capitalist = yes
			desc = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
			is_lithoid_empire = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_plant_organic = yes
			desc = civic_plant_organic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_catalytic_empire  = yes
			desc = civic_catalytic_processing
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_civic_functional_architecture = yes
			desc = civic_functional_architecture
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
			desc = gal_com_miner_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			country_uses_food = yes
			desc = gal_com_country_uses_food_no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_lithoid_empire  = yes
			desc = lithoid
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries
			desc = gal_com_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			desc = trait_nonadaptive
			owner_species = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_nonadaptive
					has_trait = trait_endemic
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_ecology_repeal_4 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_repeal_4_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
		resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries = 1
		resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_civic_expansionist = yes
			desc = gal_com_expansion_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_environmentalist = yes
			desc = gal_com_environment_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			country_uses_food = yes
			is_pacifist = yes
			is_xenophobe = no
			is_capitalist = no
			is_civic_mining_guilds = no
			desc = gal_com_opposing_ethics
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
			desc = eco_trait_clean 
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
			desc = eco_trait_dirty
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board
			desc = gal_com_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_capitalist = yes
			desc = auth_corporate
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
			is_lithoid_empire = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			is_lithoid_empire  = yes
			desc = lithoid
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_plant_organic = yes
			desc = civic_plant_organic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
			desc = gal_com_farming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_catalytic_empire  = yes
			desc = civic_catalytic_processing
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_ascension_perk = ap_arcology_project
				is_civic_terraformer = yes
			}
			NOR = {
				has_ascension_perk = ap_world_shaper
				is_civic_environmentalist = yes
				is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
				has_origin = origin_life_seeded
			}
			desc = gal_com_terraforming_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ascension_perk = ap_hydrocentric
			desc = ap_hydrocentric
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_civic_functional_architecture = yes
			desc = civic_functional_architecture
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
			desc = gal_com_miner_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			country_uses_food = yes
			desc = gal_com_country_uses_food_no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_lithoid_empire  = yes
			desc = lithoid
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			desc = trait_nonadaptive
			owner_species = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_nonadaptive
					has_trait = trait_endemic
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_monthly_income = { resource = minerals  value < 50 }
			desc = gal_com_mineral_income
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys  value < 25 }
			desc = gal_com_mineral_income
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_deficit = minerals
			desc = gal_com_mineral_income
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_deficit = alloys
			desc = gal_com_alloy_income
		}
	}
}

			in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens

	icon = "GFX_resolution_ecological_protection"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
		resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries = 1
		resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens = 1
		resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board = 1
		resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = ecology_pops_patch_flag }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative_tooltip_2
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_global_flag = ecology_pops_patch_flag
					OR = {
						has_policy_flag = eco_policy_environmental_selfregulation
						has_policy_flag = eco_policy_environmental_exploitation
						has_policy_flag = eco_policy_environmental_deregulation
						has_policy_flag = eco_environmental_policy_default
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = diploevent.3 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board"
	}
	
	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = ecology_pops_patch_flag
				has_policy_flag = eco_environmental_policy_default
			}
		}
	}

resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_studies"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions

			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_xenoist days = 7200 }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							can_set_ai_policy = yes
							has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
						}

						AND = {
							has_met_primitives = yes
							has_policy_flag = interference_passive
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10100 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				can_set_ai_policy = yes
				has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
			}

			AND = {
				has_met_primitives = yes
				has_policy_flag = interference_passive

	}

		}

			desc = ethic_materialist
			is_xenophile = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
			}
			desc = gal_com_supporting_civics
			is_xenophile = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = no
			is_spiritualist = no
			any_planet_within_border = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_observing_primitives
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_system_within_border = {
				any_fleet_in_system = {
					exists = owner

			}
			desc = gal_com_enclave_in_borders

resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_studies"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_progressive days = 7200 }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_technology = tech_selected_lineages
							has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_natural_selection
						}

						AND = {
							has_technology = tech_capacity_boosters
							NOT = { has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_capacity_boosters }
						}
						
						AND = {
							has_global_flag = expanded_megastructures_installed
							has_technology = tech_selected_lineages_machine
							NOT = { has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_selected_lineages_machine }
						}
						
						AND = {
							has_global_flag = expanded_megastructures_installed
							has_technology = tech_capacity_boosters_machine
							NOT = { has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_capacity_boosters_machine }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10110 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies
			AND = {
				has_technology = tech_selected_lineages

# THE GREATER GOOD

resolution_greatergood_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_veto"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_progressive days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_ethical_hedonism
			}
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			desc = civic_machine_servitor
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_has_elite  = yes
			desc = gal_com_elite_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
			desc = gal_com_meritocracy_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_pleasure_seeker = yes
			desc = civic_pleasure_seekers
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
			desc = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_free_haven = yes
			desc = civic_free_haven
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = { is_inwards_perfection_empire = yes is_pompous_empire = yes }
			desc = civic_inwards_perfection
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				has_slaver_civic = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			}
			desc = gal_com_slaver_empire
		}
	}
}

			is_authoritarian = yes

		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian

		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {

		}
	}

				limit = { is_authoritarian = no }

resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		AND = {
			has_global_flag = expanded_pops_active
			has_policy_flag = no_union_rights
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = expanded_pops_active }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_workers_rights_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
				every_playable_country = {
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						is_gestalt = no
						has_policy_flag = no_union_rights
					}
					country_event = { id = diploevent.4 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_slaver_civic = yes
						is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
						is_slaver = yes
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_totalitarian days = 7200 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_ethical_hedonism
			}
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_has_elite  = yes
			desc = gal_com_elite_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
			desc = gal_com_meritocracy_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_pleasure_seeker = yes
			desc = civic_pleasure_seekers
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			desc = gal_com_slaver_empire
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_capitalist = yes
			desc = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_civic_shared_burden = yes
			desc = civic_shared_burden

		modifier = {

			OR = { is_inwards_perfection_empire = yes is_pompous_empire = yes }

resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 2

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_slaver_civic = yes
						is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
						is_slaver = yes
						allows_slavery = yes
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_totalitarian days = 7200 }
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					is_gestalt = no
					any_owned_species = {
						is_sapient = yes
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10200 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_workers_rights
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes

resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves_tooltip

		hidden_effect = {
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = federations.10010 days = 15 }
			}

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes

					OR = {
						any_enslaved_species = {
							is_sapient = yes
							OR = {
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_normal country = prev  }
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_livestock country = prev }
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_matrix country = prev }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = no
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_dystopian_society country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10210 }
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { 
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_origin = origin_broken_shackles 
				}
				country_event = { id = origin.5095 }
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_totalitarian days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		every_playable_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				has_origin = origin_broken_shackles 
			}
			country_event = { id = origin.5100 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_workers_rights
			any_enslaved_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_normal country = prev }
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_livestock country = prev }
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_matrix country = prev }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_dystopian_society country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_ethical_hedonism

		}

			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_slaver_civic = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_dystopian_society country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_slaver_empire
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_capitalist = yes
			desc = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_egalitarian = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_ethical_hedonism
			}
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			desc = ethic_xenophile
			is_authoritarian = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_civic_shared_burden = yes
			desc = civic_shared_burden
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			desc = civic_machine_servitor
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_agrarian_empire = { allow_invalid = yes }
			desc = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_free_haven = yes
			desc = civic_free_haven
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5

			desc = civic_inwards_perfection

resolution_mutualdefense_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_red"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_mutualdefense_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_mutualdefense_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_imperialist days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_mutualdefense_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_war
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_militarist = yes
				is_civic_militarist = yes
			}
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			OR = { is_inwards_perfection_empire = yes is_pompous_empire = yes }
			desc = civic_inwards_perfection
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			desc = gal_com_diplo_civic
		}
	}
}

resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_mutual_defense"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_mutualdefense days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_prosperity days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_isolationist days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_mutualdefense days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_enemy_of_my_enemy"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_proclamation"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_renegade_containment"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_loved
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_war
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			desc = gal_com_military_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			desc = gal_com_diplo_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_free_traders = yes
			desc = gal_com_trade_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.5
			is_militarist = no
			desc = gal_com_low_naval_capacity_percent
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			used_naval_capacity_percent > 0.8
			is_pacifist = no
			desc = gal_com_high_naval_capacity_percent
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
	}
}

resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_mutual_defense"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 2

	modifier = {
		resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield = 1
		resolution_mutualdefense_naval_weight = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_mutualdefense days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_prosperity days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_isolationist days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = { set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_mutualdefense days = @resolution_flag_timer } }
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.5
		is_subject = no
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			desc = gal_com_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			in_breach_of = resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			desc = gal_com_military_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			desc = gal_com_diplo_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_free_traders = yes
			desc = gal_com_trade_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.5
			desc = gal_com_low_naval_capacity_percent
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_war
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
	}
}

resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_denouncement = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_mutual_defense"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	valid_target = {
		is_playable = yes
		NOT = { is_same_value = from } # don't denounce yourself.
		OR = {
			is_galactic_community_member = no
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			opinion_level = { who = from level < neutral }
			from = { is_rival = prev }
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			imperial_authority <= 100
		}
	}

	effect = {
		add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_denounced days = 3600 }
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_proclamation"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_renegade_containment"
		}
	}

	allow = {
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 75
			desc = gal_com_target_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 50
			desc = gal_com_target_emperor
		}
		# Never on yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_me
		}
		# More likely against rival
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_rival = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_at_war_with = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
	}
}

resolution_council_denouncement = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_purges"

	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_federations_dlc = yes
			has_nemesis = yes
		}
		is_galactic_council_established = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished }
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	valid_target = {
		is_playable = yes
		is_galactic_community_member = yes
		NOT = { is_same_value = from } # don't denounce yourself.
		OR = {
			opinion_level = { who = from level < neutral }
			from = { is_rival = prev }
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			imperial_authority <= 100
		}
	}

	effect = {
		add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_denounced days = 3600 }
	}

	allow = {
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 75
			desc = gal_com_target_emperor
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 50
			desc = gal_com_target_emperor
		}
		# Never on yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_me
		}
		# More likely against rival
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_rival = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_at_war_with = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
		
		# weaklings are scared of BtC
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_nemesis = yes
			any_playable_country = {
				#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
				OR = {
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
				}
				NOT = { is_same_value = prev }
				has_resource = {
					type = menace
					amount > 1000
				}
				relative_power = {
					who = prev
					category = all
					value > equivalent
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_afraid_of_powerful_crisis
		}

		# everyone is scared of BtC
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_nemesis = yes
			any_playable_country = {
				#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
				OR = {
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
				}
				NOT = { is_same_value = prev }
				has_resource = {
					type = menace
					amount > 2000
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_afraid_of_crisis
		}

		# imagine having a BtC empire next door
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_nemesis = yes
			any_neighbor_country = {
				#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
				OR = {
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_afraid_of_neighbor_crisis
		}

		# imagine your rival having a (not too scary) BtC empire next door - that's good
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			has_nemesis = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
					OR = {
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
					}
				}
			}
			any_rival_country = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
					#has_crisis_level < crisis_level_5
					OR = {
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
						#has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_pleased_to_have_rival_neighboring_crisis
		}
	}
}


# RULES OF WAR

resolution_rulesofwar_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_red"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_prosperity days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_isolationist days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular	
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			desc = gal_com_military_civic
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace
			desc = personality_vb_keepers_of_peace
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_open_gestalt = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_inwards_perfection_empire = yes
				is_pompous_empire = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_opposing_civics
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_pacifist = yes
			desc = ethic_pacifist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
			desc = ap_become_the_crisis
		}
	}
}

			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			desc = gal_com_military_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			desc = gal_com_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}

			}
		}
		
		modifier = {

				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_inwards_perfection_empire = yes
				is_pompous_empire = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_opposing_civics
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_xenophile = yes

resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_rules_of_war"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 2

	modifier = {
		resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_imperialist days = 7200 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_ai_personality_behaviour = purger
						AND = {
							is_current_or_former_necrophage_empire = yes
							is_pacifist = no
							is_xenophobic_isolationists = no
						}
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_supremacist days = 7200 }
			}

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10300 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			has_country_flag = resolution_breached_fired_cracker
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_popular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = { has_civic = civic_living_hosts is_current_or_former_necrophage_empire = yes }
			is_pacifist = no
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = no
			desc = origin_necrophage
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace
			desc = personality_vb_keepers_of_peace
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
		}
				
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			desc = gal_com_military_civic
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			desc = gal_com_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
			desc = gal_com_ally_in_breach_of_proposed_resolution
			any_federation_ally = {

					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }

				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life

		}

		modifier = {

			has_ai_personality_behaviour = purger

		resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = 1

	}

	effect = {

		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_independent_tribunals_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_imperialist days = 7200 }
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_supremacist days = 7200 }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					OR = {
						has_policy_flag = orbital_bombardment_armageddon
						has_policy_flag = orbital_bombardment_indiscriminate
						has_policy_flag = orbital_bombardment_redtoxin

	}

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }

	}

	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
			has_policy_flag = orbital_bombardment_armageddon
			has_policy_flag = orbital_bombardment_indiscriminate
			has_country_flag = resolution_breached_fired_neutron

resolution_divinity_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_divinity_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_divinity_comfort_the_fallen"
			remove_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_divinity_comfort_the_fallen
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_divinity_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_traditionalist days = 7200 }
			if = {
				limit = { is_civic_shared_burden = yes }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_progressive days = 7200 }
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_divinity_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_divinity_comfort_the_fallen"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
			is_spiritualist = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_capitalist = yes
			is_spiritualist = no
			desc = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_origin = origin_shroud_pact
			desc = origin_shroud_pact
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_gestalt = yes
			desc = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_synthetic_empire = yes
			desc = ap_synthetic_evolution
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			is_spiritualist = yes
			desc = ethic_spiritualist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
			desc = ethic_spiritualist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_shared_burden = yes
			desc = civic_shared_burden
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			count_owned_pop = {
				limit = {
					is_unemployed = yes
				}
				count > 5
			}
			desc = gal_com_unemployment
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = decadent_technocracy
				has_ai_personality = decadent_hierarchy
			}
			desc = gal_com_supporting_personality
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_materialist = no
			is_robot_empire = no
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = ai_invasion_ongoing
				has_global_flag = ai_invasion_defeated
			}
			desc = gal_com_wary_of_contingency
		}
	}
}

resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_robots_bad"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_divinity_comfort_the_fallen = 1
		resolution_divinity_tithe_on_the_soulless = 1
		resolution_divinity_right_to_work = 1
		resolution_divinity_silence_the_soulless = 1
		resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_technologist days = 7200 }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					in_breach_of = resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10340 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = resolution_ascension_cyborg_flag }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_repeal_ascension_cyborg_effect_success
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_global_flag = resolution_ascension_cyborg_flag
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_divinity_silence_the_soulless"
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = constitutional_immunity }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_synthetic_empire = no
				has_policy_flag = ai_full_rights
			}
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = synthetic_empire }
				NOT = { is_servitor_empire = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = synthetic_empire
				OR = {
					any_owned_species = {
						is_sapient = yes
						is_robotic = no
						OR = {
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_dystopian_society country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_good country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_decadent country = prev }
						}
					}
					any_owned_species = {
						is_sapient = yes
						is_robotic = no
						has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_tech_assimilation country = prev }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_loved
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 30
			has_origin = origin_shroud_pact
			desc = origin_shroud_pact
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
			NOT = { is_servitor_empire = yes }
			desc = personality_type_robot_exploiter
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			NOT = { is_servitor_empire = yes }
			desc = personality_type_robot_liberator
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes
			desc = ethic_gestalt_consciousness

		}

			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }

				is_synthetic_empire = yes

			}

		modifier = {

				has_ascension_perk = ap_organo_machine_interfacing_assimilator
				has_ascension_perk = ap_synthetic_evolution
			}

		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticreforms_form_council_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_council_size = 3
			set_council_veto = no
			remove_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished
			set_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed

			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed # council denouncement

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galcom_resolution_passed_anti_isolationist days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_loved
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_supporting_civics
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.75
			OR = {
				galactic_community_rank <= 3
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						galactic_community_rank <= 3
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_empire_or_overlord_likely_council_candidate
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_authoritarian = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = subjugator
			}
			galactic_community_rank <= 3
			desc = gal_com_empire_or_overlord_likely_council_candidate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_supporting_ethics
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			desc = personality_xenophobic_isolationists
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			galactic_community_rank > 5
			NAND = {
				is_subject = yes
				overlord = {
					opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }

	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		set_council_size = 5

		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {

		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			num_council_positions = 4
			OR = {
				galactic_community_rank = 5
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						galactic_community_rank = 5
					}
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_wants_to_add_themselves_or_overlord_to_council
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			num_council_positions = 4
			galactic_community_rank = 5
			desc = gal_com_wants_to_add_themselves_or_overlord_to_council
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			is_egalitarian = no
			desc = gal_com_negative_sentiment
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			desc = gal_com_diplo_civic
		}

resolution_galacticreforms_permanent_seat = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_member_permanent"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		is_galactic_council_established = yes
		has_galactic_emperor = no
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = no
	valid_target = {
		is_playable = yes
		is_galactic_community_member = yes
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
		is_permanent_councillor = no
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		add_permanent_councillor = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_disliked
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			is_egalitarian = yes
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
			NOT = { is_same_value = from }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = ethic_egalitarian
			NOT = { is_same_value = from }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_authoritarian = yes
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
			desc = ethic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			desc = gal_com_on_galatic_council
		}
		# More likely to vote for yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_same_value = from
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
			desc = gal_com_wants_to_add_themselves_or_overlord_to_council
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_same_value = from
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			desc = gal_com_wants_to_add_themselves_or_overlord_to_council
		}
		# Never vote for your rival
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_rival = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_at_war_with = from
			desc = gal_com_target_is_rival
		}
	}
}

resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}
	target = no
	fire_and_forget = yes

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			cancel_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_in_breach
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_federation_member_in_breach_or_denounced
		}

		modifier = {

				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_rival_in_breach_or_denounced
		}
	}

			desc = gal_com_is_in_breach
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_federation_member_in_breach_or_denounced
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_rival_in_breach_or_denounced
		}
	}
}


resolution_sanctions_tech_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_sanctions_blue"
	level = 1

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = sanctions_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			set_timed_global_flag = { flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed years = 10 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_sanctions_tech = 1
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "requires_something_illegal"
			has_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_2"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_3"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			desc = gal_com_is_in_breach
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			has_global_flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed
			desc = gal_com_recent_sanction_passed
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			desc = ethic_materialist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_federation_member_in_breach_or_denounced
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_rival_in_breach_or_denounced
		}
	}

		}

# GALACTIC FOCUS RESOLUTIONS

resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emergency_measure"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_end_game = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn_effect_success

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting

			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_contingency
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_nanites

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = ongoing_prethoryn_invasion
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn }
	}

	allow = {
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		has_global_flag = ongoing_prethoryn_invasion
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_modifier = prepared_for_the_end
			desc = ap_defender_of_the_galaxy
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_country_type = swarm
			}
			desc = gal_com_is_neighboring_swarm
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_is_neighboring_swarm
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				has_defensive_pact = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_is_neighboring_swarm
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_rival_is_neighboring_swarm
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			desc = gal_com_is_not_neighboring_swarm
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_1
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2

			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_3
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 15

			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
			desc = gal_com_crisis_stage_4
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 50

			has_ascension_perk = ap_defender_of_the_galaxy
			desc = ap_defender_of_the_galaxy
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_supporting_civics
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				is_inwards_perfection_empire = yes
				is_pompous_empire = yes
			}
			desc = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			
			is_militarist = yes
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
			desc = ethic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_xenophile = yes
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			desc = ethic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
			desc = ethic_pacifist
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_xenophobe = yes
				is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			desc = ethic_xenophobe
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			OR = {
				is_servitor_empire = yes
				is_open_gestalt = yes
			}
			desc = gal_com_supporting_civics
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			desc = gal_com_councilor
			any_country = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			desc = gal_com_custodian
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			desc = gal_com_emperor
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			}
		}
	}
}
